 The Delhi High Court has sought a reply from the Delhi government on the parole petition for treatment of former Chief Minister Om Prakash Chautala and his son Ajay Chautala, who are serving 10-year sentence in Haryana's teacher recruitment scam case
 nyaayamurti pratibha rani ne dilli sarkaar se kaha ki chautaala pita-putr kii atirikt arji par 29 janvari se pehle sthiti report pesh kii jaae

 shuru main 82 varshiya omprakash chautaala ne apane polio se grast pairon sambandhi samasya ke upachaar ke liye 60 din kii perol maangi thi
 Now Ajay has also requested a 12-week parole for 'treatment and maintaining social relationships'

 The comments hai court ne 5 march, 2015 ko is maamle main chautaala pita-putr or teen anya doshiyon kii 10-10 saal kii sajaa barkaraar rakhte hue kaha tha ki record main uplabdh sakshya hatprabh karne vaale hai
 On 16 January 2013, Chautala and 53 other convicts were convicted by the trial court in a 2000 Haryana scam in recruitment of 3206 junior basic teachers
 is maamle main bhartiya prashasnic seva ke do adhikariyon ko bhi doshi tehraaya gaya he

 is maamle main hai court ke faisle ke khilaaf pita-putr kii apil pichley saal 3 agast ko supreme court ne khaarij kar di thi
 Initially, 82-year-old Omprakash Chautala had sought a 60-day parole for treatment of foot problems related to his polio

 Researchers found that two of these drugs - vorinostat and trichostatin A, reduce the amount of calcium and magnesium in the urine

 Jianghui Hou, assistant professor of medicine science at the St
